Modifiers Appendix</p><!--]--></a><!----></div><!----></div><div class="VPSidebarItem level-1 is-link" data-v-0009425e data-v-0009425e><div class="item" data-v-0009425e><div class="indicator" data-v-0009425e></div><a class="VPLink link vp-external-link-icon link" href="https://github.com/SigmaHQ/sigma-specification/blob/main/appendix/sigma-tags-appendix.md" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" data-v-0009425e><!--[--><p class="text" data-v-0009425e>Sigma Tags Appendix</p><!--]--></a><!----></div><!----></div><div class="VPSidebarItem level-1 is-link" data-v-0009425e data-v-0009425e><div Taxonomy Appendix</p><!--]--></a><!----></div><!----></div><div class="VPSidebarItem level-1 is-link" data-v-0009425e data-v-0009425e><div class="item" data-v-0009425e><div class="indicator" data-v-0009425e></div><a class="VPLink link vp-external-link-icon link" href="https://github.com/SigmaHQ/sigma-specification/tree/main/sigmahq" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" data-v-0009425e><!--[--><p class="text" data-v-0009425e>SigmaHQ Conventions</p><!--]--></a><!----></div><!----></div><!--]--></div></section></div><!--]--><!--[--><!--[--><div class="block w-full border-t border-[var(--vp-c-divider)] pt-6 text-xs text-slate-400 transition-all dark:text-slate-700"><div class="mb-0.5 font-semibold"> Copyright © <a href="https://sigmahq.io/">SigmaHQ</a> target="_blank">Discord</a></div></div><!--]--><!--]--></nav></aside><div class="VPContent has-sidebar" id="VPContent" data-v-d8b57b2d data-v-9a6c75ad><div class="VPDoc has-sidebar has-aside" data-v-9a6c75ad data-v-e6f2a212><!--[--><!--]--><div class="container" data-v-e6f2a212><div class="aside" data-v-e6f2a212><div class="aside-curtain" data-v-e6f2a212></div><div class="aside-container" data-v-e6f2a212><div class="aside-content" data-v-e6f2a212><div class="VPDocAside" data-v-e6f2a212 data-v-cb998dce><!--[--><!--]--><!--[--><!--]--><nav aria-labelledby="doc-outline-aria-label" class="VPDocAsideOutline" data-v-cb998dce data-v-f610f197><div class="content" data-v-f610f197><div class="outline-marker" data-v-f610f197></div><div aria-level="2" class="outline-title" id="doc-outline-aria-label" role="heading" data-v-f610f197>On this page</div><ul class="VPDocOutlineItem root" data-v-f610f197 data-v-53c99d69><!--[--><!--]--></ul></div></nav><!--[--><!--]--><div class="spacer" data-v-cb998dce></div><!--[--><!--]--><!----><!--[--><!--]--><!--[--><!--]--></div></div></div></div><div class="content" data-v-e6f2a212><div class="content-container" data-v-e6f2a212><!--[--><!--]--><main class="main" data-v-e6f2a212><div style="position:relative;" class="vp-doc _docs_basics_rules" data-v-e6f2a212><div><h1 id="sigma-frontmatter-title" tabindex="-1">Sigma Rules <a class="header-anchor" href="#sigma-frontmatter-title" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;Sigma {{ $frontmatter.title }}&quot;">​</a></h1><p>Sigma rules are <code>YAML</code> files that contain all the information required to detect odd, bad or malicious behaviour when inspecting log files – usually within the context of a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Security_information_and_event_management?useskin=vector" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer">SIEM</a>.</p><p>To make the most out of the Sigma rules, it is important to understand how Sigma rules are used in detection, what all the different fields mean, and how to start writing and sharing your own Sigma detection rules.</p><div class="tip custom-block"><p class="custom-block-title">Are you new to Sigma?</p><p>If you&#39;re unfamiliar with what the Sigma Detection format is, or why it might be useful, visit the <a href="/docs/guide/about.html">About Sigma</a> page to learn more about the project &amp; available toolsets.</p></div><h2 id="starting-example" tabindex="-1">Starting Example <a class="header-anchor" href="#starting-example" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;Starting Example&quot;">​</a></h2><p>Below shows a full example of an in-use Sigma rule. <br>This example detects an &quot;Okta User Account Locked Out&quot; event. <sup class="footnote-ref"><a href="#fn1" id="fnref1">[1]</a></sup></p><div class="language-yaml vp-adaptive-theme line-numbers-mode"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">yaml</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D;"># ./rules/cloud/okta/okta_user_account_locked_out.yml</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">title</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">Okta User Account Locked Out</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">id</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">14701da0-4b0f-4ee6-9c95-2ffb4e73bb9a</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">status</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">test</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">description</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">Detects when a user account is locked out.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">references</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">    - </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">https://developer.okta.com/docs/reference/api/system-log/</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">    - </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">https://developer.okta.com/docs/reference/api/event-types/</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">author</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">Austin Songer @austinsonger</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">date</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">2021-09-12</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">modified</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">2022-10-09</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">tags</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">    - </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">attack.impact</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">logsource</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">    product</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">okta</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">    service</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">okta</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">detection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">    selection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">        displaymessage</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">Max sign in attempts exceeded</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">    condition</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">selection</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">falsepositives</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">    - </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">Unknown</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">level</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">medium</span></span></code></pre><div class="line-numbers-wrapper" aria-hidden="true"><span class="line-number">1</span><br><span class="line-number">2</span><br><span class="line-number">3</span><br><span class="line-number">4</span><br><span class="line-number">5</span><br><span class="line-number">6</span><br><span class="line-number">7</span><br><span class="line-number">8</span><br><span class="line-number">9</span><br><span class="line-number">10</span><br><span class="line-number">11</span><br><span class="line-number">12</span><br><span class="line-number">13</span><br><span class="line-number">14</span><br><span class="line-number">15</span><br><span class="line-number">16</span><br><span class="line-number">17</span><br><span class="line-number">18</span><br><span class="line-number">19</span><br><span class="line-number">20</span><br><span class="line-number">21</span><br><span class="line-number">22</span><br><span class="line-number">23</span><br></div></div><h3 id="components" tabindex="-1">Components <a class="header-anchor" href="#components" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;Components&quot;">​</a></h3><p>To help understand what the above code snippet accomplishes, this Sigma rule will be separated into three main components:</p><ul><li><strong><a href="#detection">Detection</a></strong><br><em>What malicious behaviour the rule searching for.</em></li><li><strong><a href="#logsources">Logsource</a></strong><br><em>What types of logs this detection should search over.</em></li><li><strong><a href="#metadata">Metadata</a></strong><br><em>Other information about the detection.</em></li></ul><h2 id="detection" tabindex="-1">Detection <a class="header-anchor" href="#detection" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;Detection&quot;">​</a></h2><span class="VPBadge danger relative -top-2"><!--[-->Required<!--]--></span><p>The detection section is the most important component of any Sigma rule. It specifies exactly what the rule is looking for across relevant logs.</p><div class="language-yaml vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">yaml</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark has-focused-lines vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">    product</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">okta</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">    service</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">okta</span></span>
<span class="line has-focus"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">detection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span></span>
<span class="line has-focus"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">    selection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line has-focus"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">        displaymessage</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">Max sign in attempts exceeded</span></span>
<span class="line has-focus"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">    condition</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">selection</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">falsepositives</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">    - </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">Unknown</span></span></code></pre></div><p>This specific detection above is searching for anywhere an Okta User&#39;s account has been locked out, due to the maximum number of sign-in attempts being reached.</p><h3 id="principles" tabindex="-1">Principles <a class="header-anchor" href="#principles" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;Principles&quot;">​</a></h3><p>The Sigma detection format can be quite daunting and confusing for newcomers, as some Sigma rules can be complex in how they construct detections. It&#39;s important to understand the following guiding principles:</p><h4 id="selections" tabindex="-1">Selections <a class="header-anchor" href="#selections" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;Selections&quot;">​</a></h4><p>Each Sigma detection is categorised &amp; split up into groups called &quot;<code>selections</code>&quot;. Each &quot;<code>selection</code>&quot; contains the definition for the detection itself.</p><div class="language-yaml vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">yaml</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark has-focused-lines vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">detection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line has-focus"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  selection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span></span>
<span class="line has-focus"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">    displaymessage</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">Max sign in attempts exceeded</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  condition</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">selection</span></span></code></pre></div><p>Sigma use &quot;selection&quot; groups to organise detections for readability &amp; filtering, which becomes important when exploring <a href="/docs/basics/conditions.html">Conditions</a>.</p><h4 id="and-or" tabindex="-1">And / Or <a class="header-anchor" href="#and-or" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;And / Or&quot;">​</a></h4><p>The other main consideration, is that Sigma completes <strong>&quot;AND&quot;</strong> and <strong>&quot;OR&quot;</strong> operations by using YAML Lists and Dictionaries.</p><ul><li>The <code>list</code> syntax to represent an <strong>&quot;OR&quot;</strong> operation, and</li></ul><div class="language-yaml vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">yaml</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">detection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  selection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">    field_name</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">      - </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">this</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D;"> # or</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">      - </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">that</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  condition</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">selection</span></span></code></pre></div><ul><li>The <code>dictionary</code>/<code>object</code> syntax to represent an <strong>&quot;AND&quot;</strong> operation.</li></ul><div class="language-yaml vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">yaml</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">detection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  selection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">    field_name</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">this</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D;"> # and</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">    other_field_name</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">that</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  condition</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">selection</span></span></code></pre></div><h4 id="detection-methods" tabindex="-1">Detection Methods <a class="header-anchor" href="#detection-methods" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;Detection Methods&quot;">​</a></h4><p>With both of those topics in mind, explore below on how Sigma composes detections with 3 main patterns.</p><ul><li><a href="#detection-keyword">by Keyword</a></li><li><a href="#detection-and">by Field Value</a></li><li><a href="#detection-or">by Multiple Field Values (List)</a></li></ul><h3 id="detection-keyword" tabindex="-1">by Keyword <a class="header-anchor" href="#detection-keyword" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;by Keyword {#detection-keyword}&quot;">​</a></h3><p>One of the most basic and easy-to-understand ways to detect malicious behaviour using Sigma is by using keywords. <strong>Keyword</strong>-based searches look over a given logsource for any text matching any of the provided keywords. This corresponds to searching for a string into the raw log.</p><p>Each item in the &quot;<code>keywords</code>&quot; list is effectively separated by a logical <strong>&quot;OR&quot;</strong> operator.</p><p>The below example Sigma rule uses a keyword-based search to detect when users might be covering their tracks – by purging that user&#39;s <code>.bash_history</code>.</p><div class="sigma-converter not-prose my-8" data-v-b4727905><div class="sigma-converter-static" style="" data-v-b4727905><!--[--><div class="language-yaml vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">yaml</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark has-focused-lines vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">title</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">Bash History Tampering</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">logsource</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  product</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">linux</span></span>
<span class="line has-focus"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">detection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span></span>
<span class="line has-focus"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  keywords</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line has-focus"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">    - </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;rm *bash_history&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line has-focus"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">    - </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&#39;echo &quot;&quot; &gt; *bash_history&#39;</span></span>
<span class="line has-focus"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">    - </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;truncate -s0 *bash_history&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line has-focus"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">    - </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;history -c&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line has-focus"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">    - </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;history -w&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line has-focus"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  condition</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">keywords</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">falsepositives</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">  - </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">Unknown</span></span></code></pre></div><div class="language-splunk vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">splunk</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;rm *bash_history&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> OR</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;"> &quot;echo \&quot;\&quot; &gt; *bash_history&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> OR</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;"> &quot;truncate -s0 *bash_history&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> OR</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;"> &quot;history -c&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> OR</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;"> &quot;history -w&quot;</span></span></code></pre></div><!--]--></div><!----></div><p>This example tells Sigma to generate a SIEM query that searches for any of the following keywords:</p><ul><li><code>rm *bash_history</code> <i class="opacity-50 pl-2">or</i></li><li><code>echo &quot;&quot; &gt; *bash_history</code> <i class="opacity-50 pl-2">or</i></li><li><code>truncate -s0 *bash_history</code> <i class="opacity-50 pl-2">or</i></li><li><code>history -c</code> <i class="opacity-50 pl-2">or</i></li><li><code>history -w</code></li></ul><br><div class="info custom-block"><p class="custom-block-title">Naming of <code>keywords</code></p><p>The naming of the field &quot;<code>keywords</code>&quot; under the <code>detection</code> and <code>selection</code> fields in this example is arbitrary. However, you should use it as a standard when creating your own Sigma rules.</p></div><p>When we convert the rule into Splunk Query Language (for example) using <a href="https://github.com/SigmaHQ/sigma-cli" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer">the <code>sigma-cli</code> tool</a>, the resulting query after conversion will be the following.</p><div class="language-splunk vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">splunk</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;rm *bash_history&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> OR</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;"> &quot;echo \&quot;\&quot; &gt; *bash_history&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> OR</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;"> &quot;truncate -s0 *bash_history&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> OR</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;"> &quot;history -c&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> OR</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;"> &quot;history -w&quot;</span></span></code></pre></div><div class="warning custom-block"><p class="custom-block-title">A note on efficiency</p><p>Keep in mind that while keyword-based searches are easy to write, most SIEMs will usually perform vastly better when using <a href="#detection-and">field-based searches</a>.</p></div><hr><h3 id="detection-and" tabindex="-1">by Field <a class="header-anchor" href="#detection-and" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;by Field {#detection-and}&quot;">​</a></h3><p>Next, Sigma rules can also be used to complete field-value searches.</p><p>To do this, represent the fields as a YAML &quot;object&quot; with their respective names and values.</p><div class="language-yaml vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">yaml</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">detection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  selection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">    Username</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;Administrator&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  condition</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">selection</span></span></code></pre></div><p>You can also see where <strong>multiple</strong> fields appear together, by adding more field-value pairs to the YAML object.</p><p>For instance, to detect when a USB device is inserted into a machine, you may need to consider the following events triggered within the Windows Event Logging system:</p><ul><li><a href="https://www.ultimatewindowssecurity.com/securitylog/encyclopedia/event.aspx?eventid=6416" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer"><code>EventID: 6416</code></a> A new external device was recognised by the system <i class="opacity-50 pl-1"> and</i></li><li>where the class of drive was a &quot;DiskDrive&quot;</li></ul><p>To search for where both of these occur, place both together within the <code>selection</code> object, as shown below.</p><p>The resulting query after conversion will be the following <br><i class="opacity-50">(Splunk Query Language used as an example):</i></p><div class="sigma-converter not-prose my-8" data-v-b4727905><div class="sigma-converter-static" style="" data-v-b4727905><!--[--><div class="language-yaml vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">yaml</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark has-focused-lines vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">title</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">External Disk Drive Or USB Storage Device</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">description</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">  Detects external diskdrives or plugged in USB devices,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">  EventID 6416 on windows 10 or later</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">logsource</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  product</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">windows</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  service</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">security</span></span>
<span class="line has-focus"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">detection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span></span>
<span class="line has-focus"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  selection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line has-focus"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">    EventID</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">6416</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D;"> # and where</span></span>
<span class="line has-focus"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">    ClassName</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;DiskDrive&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line has-focus"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  condition</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">selection</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">falsepositives</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">  - </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">Legitimate administrative activity</span></span></code></pre></div><div class="language-splunk vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">splunk</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">EventID</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">6416</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;"> ClassName</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;DiskDrive&quot;</span></span></code></pre></div><!--]--></div><!----></div><hr><h3 id="detection-or" tabindex="-1">by Field List <a class="header-anchor" href="#detection-or" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;by Field List {#detection-or}&quot;">​</a></h3><p>The &quot;by Field List&quot; detection method is similar to the <a href="#detection-and">&quot;by Field&quot;</a> method. It is useful when you have to search for multiple values of a field.</p><p>For example, you might want to search <code>Windows\Security</code> logs and detect when:</p><ul><li><a href="https://www.ultimatewindowssecurity.com/securitylog/encyclopedia/event.aspx?eventid=4728" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer"><code>EventID: 4728</code></a> A user is added to a Security Group (eg. Administrators) <i class="opacity-50 pl-1"> or</i></li><li><a href="https://www.ultimatewindowssecurity.com/securitylog/encyclopedia/event.aspx?eventid=4729" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer"><code>EventID: 4729</code></a> A user is removed from a Security Group <i class="opacity-50 pl-1"> or</i></li><li><a href="https://www.ultimatewindowssecurity.com/securitylog/encyclopedia/event.aspx?eventid=4730" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer"><code>EventID: 4730</code></a> A Security Group was deleted</li></ul><p>You can represent this in Sigma by using a YAML list, where each field value is prepended by a newline, followed by a &quot;<code>-</code>&quot;.</p><p>The resulting query after conversion will be the following <br><i class="opacity-50">(Splunk Query Language used as an example):</i></p><div class="sigma-converter not-prose my-8" data-v-b4727905><div class="sigma-converter-static" style="" data-v-b4727905><!--[--><div class="language-yaml vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">yaml</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark has-focused-lines vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">title</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">Group Modification Logging</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">description</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">Triggers when an account is added to or removed from any group assigned administrative privileges.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">logsource</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  product</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">windows</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  service</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">system</span></span>
<span class="line has-focus"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">detection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span></span>
<span class="line has-focus"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  selection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line has-focus"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">    EventID</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line has-focus"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">      - </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">4728</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D;"> # or where</span></span>
<span class="line has-focus"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">      - </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">4729</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D;"> # or where</span></span>
<span class="line has-focus"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">      - </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">4730</span></span>
<span class="line has-focus"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  condition</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">selection</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">falsepositives</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">  - </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">Unknown</span></span></code></pre></div><div class="language-splunk vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">splunk</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">EventID IN (</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">4728</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">,</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;"> 4729</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">,</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;"> 4730</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">)</span></span></code></pre></div><!--]--></div><!----></div><h3 id="conditions" tabindex="-1">Conditions <a class="header-anchor" href="#conditions" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;Conditions&quot;">​</a></h3><p>The Sigma <code>detection</code> section can consist of one or more detections, or &quot;selection&quot; groups. Each selection group must be present in the condition field at the bottom of the detection section.</p><p>The default name given to this group is <code>selection</code>, but it is often given more descriptive information about what it&#39;s attempting to detect.</p><div class="language-yaml vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">yaml</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">detection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  selection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">    field</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">value</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  condition</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">selection</span></span></code></pre></div><div class="info custom-block"><p class="custom-block-title">Conditions</p><p>It&#39;s worth noting that conditions can be used to organize various selection groups, as well as combine or negate with other selection groups to perform powerful detection operations within the SIEM. For instance:</p><div class="language-yaml vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">yaml</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">condition</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">(selection_one or selection_two) and not filter</span></span></code></pre></div><p>If you want to learn more about combining different &quot;selection groups&quot;, <a href="/docs/basics/conditions.html">you can check out the Conditions section of the documentation</a>.</p></div><h2 id="logsources" tabindex="-1">Logsources <a class="header-anchor" href="#logsources" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;Logsources&quot;">​</a></h2><span class="VPBadge danger relative -top-2"><!--[-->Required<!--]--></span><p>The <code>logsource</code> section in Sigma rules is used to specify what log data should be searched by the rule. By specifying the appropriate log type in the logsource field, Sigma rules can target a specific variety of logs, rather than searching over all types of logs within a SIEM.</p><p>It splits up each defined logsource into three distinct fields - <code>category</code>, <code>product</code>, and <code>service</code>.</p><ul><li><strong>Category</strong><br>This describes a category of products.<br>(Eg. <code>webserver</code>, <code>firewall</code> or <code>edr</code>)<br><br></li><li><strong>Product</strong><br>This describes a specific product.<br>(Eg. <code>windows</code>, <code>linux</code>, <code>cisco</code>)<br><br></li><li><strong>Service</strong><br>This describes a service running within a given product<br>(Eg. <code>kerberos</code>, <code>defender</code> etc).<br><br></li></ul><div class="language-yaml vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">yaml</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark has-focused-lines vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">author</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">Austin Songer @austinsonger</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">date</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">2021-09-12</span></span>
<span class="line has-focus"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">logsource</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span></span>
<span class="line has-focus"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  product</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">okta</span></span>
<span class="line has-focus"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  service</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">okta</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">detection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  selection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span></code></pre></div><p>Sigma rules usually use <a href="/docs/basics/log-sources.html#standard-logsources">a standard combination</a> of these fields to target a specific log source.</p><div class="info custom-block"><p class="custom-block-title">Logsource <code>definition</code></p><p>The <code>definition</code> field within logsource can also provide more information about how to onboard the log data source correctly.</p><div class="language-yaml vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">yaml</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark has-focused-lines vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">tags</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">  - </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">attack.privilege_escalation</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">  - </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">attack.t1548</span></span>
<span class="line has-focus"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">logsource</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span></span>
<span class="line has-focus"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  product</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">windows</span></span>
<span class="line has-focus"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  category</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">ps_script</span></span>
<span class="line has-focus"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  definition</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">Script Block Logging must be enabled</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">detection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  selection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">    ScriptBlockText|contains</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;Invoke-Nightmare&quot;</span></span></code></pre></div></div><a href="/docs/basics/log-sources.html"><div class="box group relative z-10 flex h-full w-full flex-col rounded-lg bg-[#E3F2FA]/40 p-6 text-white outline outline-2 outline-[#C6D2ED]/40 transition-all hover:bg-[#DEF5FC] hover:outline-2 hover:outline-offset-2 hover:outline-[#AAD0EC] dark:bg-[#252C3B]/25 dark:outline-[#383C5E]/50 dark:hover:bg-[#37455E]/40 dark:hover:outline-[var(--vp-c-brand-1)]"><span class="box-icon mb-4 flex h-10 w-10 items-center justify-center rounded-full bg-transparent text-slate-700 outline outline-1 outline-[#C6D2ED]/70 transition-all group-hover:bg-[var(--vp-c-brand-1)] group-hover:text-white group-hover:outline-[var(--vp-c-brand-1)] dark:text-[var(--vp-c-brand-1)] dark:outline-slate-400/30 dark:group-hover:text-white"><!--[--><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="currentColor" aria-hidden="true" data-slot="icon"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M3 6.75A.75.75 0 0 1 3.75 6h16.5a.75.75 0 0 1 0 1.5H3.75A.75.75 0 0 1 3 6.75ZM3 12a.75.75 0 0 1 .75-.75H12a.75.75 0 0 1 0 1.5H3.75A.75.75 0 0 1 3 12Zm0 dark:text-white"><!--[-->Logsources<!--]--></span><span class="text-d m-0 p-0 text-sm text-[#7280A0] dark:text-slate-500"><!--[-->Learn how to tune your Sigma rules for specific sets of logs.<!--]--></span></div></a><h2 id="metadata" tabindex="-1">Metadata <a class="header-anchor" href="#metadata" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;Metadata&quot;">​</a></h2><span class="VPBadge tip relative -top-2"><!--[-->Optional<!--]--></span><p>Everything else that you can see around the <a href="#logsources">logsource</a> and <a href="#detection">detection</a> sections is what Sigma calls &quot;Metadata&quot;, and can include fields such as <code>tags</code>, <code>level</code>, <code>references</code>, <code>description</code> and more.</p><div class="info custom-block"><p class="custom-block-title">Sigma Specification</p><p>There is a <a href="https://github.com/SigmaHQ/sigma-specification/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer">defined Sigma specification</a> that outlines what Sigma considers to be &quot;standard&quot; fields, but it&#39;s important to note that Sigma rules can contain any amount of Metadata fields you like.</p></div><h3 id="available-sigma-metadata-fields" tabindex="-1">Available Sigma metadata Fields <a class="header-anchor" href="#available-sigma-metadata-fields" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;Available Sigma metadata Fields&quot;">​</a></h3><p>Below is a list of standard Sigma metadata fields.</p><ul class="columns-2 lg:columns-3 pb-8 pb-8 block"><li><a href="#metadata-title">Title</a></li><li><a href="#metadata-id">ID</a></li><li><a href="#metadata-status">Status</a></li><li><a href="#metadata-description">Description</a></li><li><a href="#metadata-license">License</a></li><li><a href="#metadata-author">Author</a></li><li><a href="#metadata-date-modified">Date / Modified</a></li><li><a href="#metadata-references">References</a></li><li><a href="#metadata-tags">Tags</a></li><li><a href="#metadata-false-positives">False Positives</a></li><li><a href="#metadata-level">Level</a></li></ul><hr><h4 id="metadata-title" tabindex="-1">Title <a class="header-anchor" href="#metadata-title" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;Title { #metadata-title }&quot;">​</a></h4><span class="VPBadge danger mt-2"><!--[-->Required<!--]--></span><p>The <code>title</code> field is used to give a very short summary of what the rule is trying to achieve.</p><div class="language-yaml vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">yaml</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">title</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">Okta User Account Locked Out</span></span></code></pre></div><div class="tip custom-block"><p class="custom-block-title">Hint on writing good Alert titles</p><p>Try to keep your alert titles as short as possible, and avoid prefixes like &quot;Detects when ...&quot;.</p></div><hr><h4 id="metadata-id" tabindex="-1">ID <a class="header-anchor" href="#metadata-id" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;ID { #metadata-id }&quot;">​</a></h4><p>The <code>id</code> field should be generated whenever you create a Sigma rule, and globally identifies the Sigma rules against all others. For this reason, Sigma recommends using randomly generated UUIDs (version 4).</p><p>You can generate your own UUIDv4 by <a href="https://www.uuidgenerator.net/version4" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer">following the link here</a>.</p><div class="language-yaml vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">yaml</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">id</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">12345678-bef0-4204-a928-ef5e620d6fcc</span></span></code></pre></div><div class="info custom-block"><p class="custom-block-title">Rule ID changes</p><p>Rule identifiers should only change for the following reasons:</p><ul><li>Major changes in the rule. (E.g. a different rule logic.)</li><li>Derivation of a new rule from an existing or refinement of a rule in a way that both are kept active.</li><li>Merge of rules.</li></ul></div><hr><h4 id="metadata-status" tabindex="-1">Status <a class="header-anchor" href="#metadata-status" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;Status { #metadata-status }&quot;">​</a></h4><p>The <code>status</code> field advertises the current state of the Sigma rules as in-development, in-testing or ready for use.</p><blockquote><p>Values: <code>stable</code> | <code>test</code> | <code>experimental</code> | <code>deprecated</code> | <code>unsupported</code></p></blockquote><div class="language-yaml vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">yaml</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">status</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">stable</span></span></code></pre></div><hr><h4 id="metadata-description" tabindex="-1">Description <a class="header-anchor" href="#metadata-description" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;Description { #metadata-description }&quot;">​</a></h4><p>The <code>description</code> field gives some explanation of the reason why the rule is in existence, how to best use it, and when it will trigger.</p><div class="language-yaml vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">yaml</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">description</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">This rule detects Windows RDP administrative logon</span></span></code></pre></div><div class="warning custom-block"><p class="custom-block-title">Writing Good Descriptions</p><p>Descriptions are often used by other products and services to help susinctly explain what the rule is trying to achieve. Try to avoid using:</p><ul><li>&quot;Detects when ...&quot; or &quot;Detects if ...&quot;</li><li>&quot;This rule will ...&quot;</li></ul></div><hr><h4 id="metadata-license" tabindex="-1">License <a class="header-anchor" href="#metadata-license" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;License { #metadata-license }&quot;">​</a></h4><span class="VPBadge info mt-2"><!--[-->Optional<!--]--></span><p>The <code>license</code> field optionally specifies a SPDX IDs reference on how the Sigma rule can be used by others within the community.</p><div class="language-yaml vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">yaml</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">license</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">MIT</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D;"># OR</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">license</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">GPL-2.0-or-later</span></span></code></pre></div><div class="warning custom-block"><p class="custom-block-title">Publishing Sigma Rules</p><p>When contributing rules to the community, some repositories will usually have a <code>LICENSE</code> file that outlines the license of the entire repository, and all the detection rules pertained inside of it.</p><p>Remember to discuss the topic of any possible conflicting licenses with the repository owner before contributing any rules.</p></div><hr><h4 id="metadata-author" tabindex="-1">Author <a class="header-anchor" href="#metadata-author" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;Author { #metadata-author }&quot;">​</a></h4><p>The <code>author</code> field specifies the singular author of the Sigma rule. It can also include a Twitter handle, email, or other way to contact the author.</p><div class="language-yaml vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">yaml</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">author</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">Sirens [sirens@sigma.hq]</span></span></code></pre></div><hr><h4 id="metadata-date-modified" tabindex="-1">Date / Modified <a class="header-anchor" href="#metadata-date-modified" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;Date / Modified { #metadata-date-modified }&quot;">​</a></h4><p>The <code>date</code> / <code>modified</code> field states the creation / last modified date of the rule.</p><div class="language-yaml vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">yaml</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">date</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">2023-01-01</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">modified</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">2023-01-02</span></span></code></pre></div><div class="info custom-block"><p class="custom-block-title">Date Format</p><p>The <code>date</code> and <code>modified</code> fields should be standardised to use the ISO 8601 date with separator format : YYYY-MM-DD.</p></div><div class="tip custom-block"><p class="custom-block-title">When to change the <code>modified</code> date?</p><p>You should only change the modified date when you:</p><ul><li>change the <code>title</code>,</li><li>change the <code>detection</code> section,</li><li>change the <code>level</code> <i class="opacity-50 pl-1">or</i></li><li>change the <code>logsource</code></li></ul></div><hr><h4 id="metadata-references" tabindex="-1">References <a class="header-anchor" href="#metadata-references" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;References { #metadata-references }&quot;">​</a></h4><p>The <code>references</code> field provides a URL, list of URLs or other text references how, or why the Sigma rule was created by the author.</p><div class="language-yaml vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">yaml</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">references</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">https://learn.microsoft.com/en-us/windows/security/threat-protection/auditing/event-6416</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D;"># OR</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">references</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">    - </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">Plain Text (Eg. CVE-2025-22222)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">    - </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">https://www.trendmicro.com/vinfo/hk-en/security/news/cybercrime-and-digital-threats/malicious-spam-campaign-uses-iso-image-files-to-deliver-lokibot-and-nanocore</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">    - </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">https://www.proofpoint.com/us/blog/threat-insight/threat-actor-profile-ta2719-uses-colorful-lures-deliver-rats-local-languages</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">    - </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">https://twitter.com/MsftSecIntel/status/1257324139515269121</span></span></code></pre></div><hr><h4 id="metadata-tags" tabindex="-1">Tags <a class="header-anchor" href="#metadata-tags" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;Tags { #metadata-tags }&quot;">​</a></h4><p>The <code>tags</code> field applies is used to categorize or map Sigma rules into a variety of different security frameworks and availability standards. These include, but are not limited to:</p><ul><li><a href="https://attack.mitre.org/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer">MITRE ATT&amp;CK Framework</a></li><li><a href="https://car.mitre.org/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer">MITRE Cyber Analytics Repository (CAR)</a></li><li><a href="https://www.cisa.gov/news-events/news/traffic-light-protocol-tlp-definitions-and-usage" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer">Traffic Light Protocol (TLP)</a></li><li><a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cve/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer">Common Vulnerabilities and Exposures (CVE)</a></li></ul><div class="language-yaml vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">yaml</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">tags</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D;">  # MITRE ATT&amp;CK framework references</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">  - </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">attack.discovery</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">  - </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">attack.t1012</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D;">  # MITRE Cyber Analytics Repository (CAR)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">  - </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">car.2016-04-005</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">  - </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">car-2016-04-005</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D;">  # Traffic Light Protocol</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">  - </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">tlp.amber</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">  - </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">tlp.green</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D;">  # CVE</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">  - </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">cve.2022-27925</span></span></code></pre></div><div class="tip custom-block"><p class="custom-block-title">Tags Naming Convention</p><p>The Sigma team have defined a tag naming convention under the Sigma Specification repository. You can find more information about this <a href="https://github.com/SigmaHQ/sigma-specification/blob/main/appendix/sigma-tags-appendix.md" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer">here on the <code>sigma-specification</code> repo</a>.</p></div><hr><h4 id="metadata-false-positives" tabindex="-1">False Positives <a class="header-anchor" href="#metadata-false-positives" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;False Positives { #metadata-false-positives }&quot;">​</a></h4><p>The <code>falsepositives</code> field outlines a list of possible known false positives that may occur.</p><div class="language-yaml vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">yaml</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">falsepositives</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">  - </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">This rule can sometimes create false-positives when a user forefully restarts their workstation</span></span></code></pre></div><div class="tip custom-block"><p class="custom-block-title">False Positives vs Filters</p><p>False-positives are not parsed by the Sigma convertors, and are simply there to help the detection-engineer or analyst to triage the alert as to when the rule might trigger in a non-malicious context.</p><p>If you want to filter out certain events, you should use the <code>condition</code> field in combination with a <code>filter</code> condition in the <code>detection</code> section, or use the <a href="/docs/meta/filters.html">newly published Sigma Filters feature</a> to help tune your alerts.</p></div><hr><h4 id="metadata-level" tabindex="-1">Level <a class="header-anchor" href="#metadata-level" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;Level { #metadata-level }&quot;">​</a></h4><p>The <code>level</code> field describes the criticality of a triggered rule.</p><p>While low and medium level events have an informative character, events with high and critical level should lead to immediate reviews by security analysts.</p><div class="language-yaml vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">yaml</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">level</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">low</span></span></code></pre></div><blockquote><p>Values: <code>critical</code> | <code>high</code> | <code>medium</code> | <code>low</code> | <code>informational</code></p></blockquote><p>The five existing levels are divided into two categories.</p><ul><li>Rules that have informative character and should be displayed in a list or bar chart<br>(<code>informational</code>,<code>low</code>, <code>medium</code>)<br><br></li><li>Rules that should trigger a dedicated alert<br>(<code>high</code>, <code>critical</code>)<br><br></li></ul><p>Apply the following guidelines when setting a level:</p><ul><li>Rules of level <code>critical</code> should never trigger a false positive and be of high relevance</li><li>Rules of level <code>high</code> trigger on threats of high relevance that have to be reviewed manually (rare false positives &gt; baselining required)</li><li>Rules of level <code>high</code> and <code>critical</code> indicate an incident (if not a false positive)</li><li>Rules of level <code>low</code> and <code>medium</code> indicate suspicious activity and policy violations</li><li>Rules of level <code>informational</code> have informative character and are often used for compliance or correlation purposes</li></ul><hr class="footnotes-sep"><section class="footnotes"><ol class="footnotes-list"><li id="fn1" class="footnote-item"><p>Rule sourced from SigmaHQ/sigma repository 8 Dec 2022: <a href="https://github.com/SigmaHQ/sigma/blob/master/rules/cloud/okta/okta_user_account_locked_out.yml" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer">https://github.com/SigmaHQ/sigma/blob/master/rules/cloud/okta/okta_user_account_locked_out.yml</a> <a href="#fnref1" class="footnote-backref">↩︎</a></p></li></ol></section></div></div></main><footer class="VPDocFooter" data-v-e6f2a212 data-v-1bcd8184><!--[--><!--]--><div class="edit-info" data-v-1bcd8184><div target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" data-v-1bcd8184><!--[--><span class="vpi-square-pen edit-link-icon" data-v-1bcd8184></span> Edit on GitHub<!--]--></a></div><div class="last-updated"
