target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" data-v-0009425e><!--[--><p class="text" data-v-0009425e>Sigma Filters</p><!--]--></a><!----></div><!----></div><div class="VPSidebarItem level-1 is-link" data-v-0009425e data-v-0009425e><div class="item" data-v-0009425e><div class="indicator" data-v-0009425e></div><a class="VPLink link vp-external-link-icon link" href="https://github.com/SigmaHQ/sigma-specification/blob/main/appendix/sigma-modifiers-appendix.md" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" data-v-0009425e><!--[--><p class="text" data-v-0009425e>Sigma Modifiers Appendix</p><!--]--></a><!----></div><!----></div><div class="VPSidebarItem level-1 is-link" data-v-0009425e data-v-0009425e><div class="item" data-v-0009425e><div class="indicator" data-v-0009425e></div><a class="VPLink link vp-external-link-icon link" href="https://github.com/SigmaHQ/sigma-specification/blob/main/appendix/sigma-tags-appendix.md" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" data-v-0009425e><!--[--><p class="text" data-v-0009425e>Sigma Tags Appendix</p><!--]--></a><!----></div><!----></div><div class="VPSidebarItem level-1 is-link" data-v-0009425e data-v-0009425e><div class="item" data-v-0009425e><div class="indicator" data-v-0009425e></div><a class="VPLink link vp-external-link-icon link" href="https://github.com/SigmaHQ/sigma-specification/blob/main/appendix/sigma-taxonomy-appendix.md" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" data-v-0009425e><!--[--><p class="text" data-v-0009425e>Sigma Taxonomy Appendix</p><!--]--></a><!----></div><!----></div><div class="VPSidebarItem level-1 is-link" data-v-0009425e data-v-0009425e><div class="item" data-v-0009425e><div class="indicator" data-v-0009425e></div><a class="VPLink link vp-external-link-icon link" href="https://github.com/SigmaHQ/sigma-specification/tree/main/sigmahq" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" data-v-0009425e><!--[--><p class="text" data-v-0009425e>SigmaHQ Conventions</p><!--]--></a><!----></div><!----></div><!--]--></div></section></div><!--]--><!--[--><!--[--><div class="block w-full border-t border-[var(--vp-c-divider)] pt-6 text-xs text-slate-400 transition-all dark:text-slate-700"><div class="mb-0.5 font-semibold"> Copyright © <a href="https://sigmahq.io/">SigmaHQ</a> 2026</div><div class="flex gap-2"><a href="https://github.com/SigmaHQ/" class="hover:text-cyan-600" target="_blank">Github</a><span class="opacity-30">|</span><a href="https://twitter.com/Sigma_HQ/" class="hover:text-cyan-600" target="_blank">X.com</a><span class="opacity-30">|</span><a href="https://discord.gg/kQQBn5W2z5" class="hover:text-cyan-600" target="_blank">Discord</a></div></div><!--]--><!--]--></nav></aside><div class="VPContent has-sidebar" id="VPContent" data-v-d8b57b2d data-v-9a6c75ad><div class="VPDoc has-sidebar has-aside" data-v-9a6c75ad data-v-e6f2a212><!--[--><!--]--><div class="container" data-v-e6f2a212><div class="aside" data-v-e6f2a212><div class="aside-curtain" data-v-e6f2a212></div><div class="aside-container" data-v-e6f2a212><div class="aside-content" data-v-e6f2a212><div class="VPDocAside" data-v-e6f2a212 data-v-cb998dce><!--[--><!--]--><!--[--><!--]--><nav aria-labelledby="doc-outline-aria-label" class="VPDocAsideOutline" data-v-cb998dce data-v-f610f197><div class="content" data-v-f610f197><div class="outline-marker" data-v-f610f197></div><div aria-level="2" class="outline-title" id="doc-outline-aria-label" role="heading" data-v-f610f197>On this page</div><ul class="VPDocOutlineItem root" data-v-f610f197 data-v-53c99d69><!--[--><!--]--></ul></div></nav><!--[--><!--]--><div class="spacer" data-v-cb998dce></div><!--[--><!--]--><!----><!--[--><!--]--><!--[--><!--]--></div></div></div></div><div class="content" data-v-e6f2a212><div class="content-container" data-v-e6f2a212><!--[--><!--]--><main class="main" data-v-e6f2a212><div style="position:relative;" class="vp-doc _docs_basics_modifiers" data-v-e6f2a212><div><h1 id="sigma-frontmatter-title" tabindex="-1">Sigma Modifiers <a class="header-anchor" href="#sigma-frontmatter-title" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;Sigma {{ $frontmatter.title }}&quot;">​</a></h1><p>Introduced in <a href="https://patzke.org/introducing-sigma-value-modifiers.html" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer">2019</a>, Sigma modifiers were incorporated into the Sigma specification, allowing detection engineers to perform more complex operations on Sigma rules. These operations, including Regex, Boolean logic, and <code>cidr</code> notation, are supported by most SIEMs.</p><h2 id="overview" tabindex="-1">Overview <a class="header-anchor" href="#overview" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;Overview&quot;">​</a></h2><p>The values of given fields contained within Sigma rules can be changed using Value Modifiers. Value modifiers (or more simply, &quot;modifiers&quot;) are appended after the field name with a pipe character <code>|</code> to each field you want to modify.</p><p><em>Example:</em></p><div class="language-yaml vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">yaml</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">detection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">    selection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line highlighted"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">        TargetFilename|endswith</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&#39;.cmdline&#39;</span></span></code></pre></div><div class="language-splunk vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">splunk</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">TargetFilename</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;*.cmdline&quot;</span></span></code></pre></div><p>Modifiers can also be chained together to perform more complex operations.</p><h2 id="available-field-modifiers" tabindex="-1">Available Field Modifiers <a class="header-anchor" href="#available-field-modifiers" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;Available Field Modifiers&quot;">​</a></h2><p>Below is a list of available field modifiers.</p><ul class="columns-2 lg:columns-3 pb-8 pb-8 block"><li><a href="#all"><code>all</code></a></li><li><a href="#base64-base64offset"><code>base64</code> / <code>base64offset</code></a></li><li><a href="#cased"><code>cased</code></a></li><li><a href="#cidr"><code>cidr</code></a></li><li><a href="#contains"><code>contains</code></a></li><li><a href="#endswith"><code>endswith</code></a></li><li><a href="#exists"><code>exists</code></a></li><li><a href="#expand"><code>expand</code></a></li><li><a href="#fieldref"><code>fieldref</code></a></li><li><a href="#gt"><code>gt</code></a></li><li><a href="#gte"><code>gte</code></a></li><li><a href="#lt"><code>lt</code></a></li><li><a href="#lte"><code>lte</code></a></li><li><a href="#re"><code>re</code></a></li><li><a href="#startswith"><code>startswith</code></a></li><li><a href="#wide"><code>utf16</code> / <code>utf16le</code> / <code>utf16be</code> / <code>wide</code></a></li><li><a href="#windash"><code>windash</code></a></li></ul><hr><h3 id="all" tabindex="-1">all <a class="header-anchor" href="#all" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;all&quot;">​</a></h3><div class="sigma-converter not-prose my-8" data-v-b4727905><div class="sigma-converter-static" style="" data-v-b4727905><!--[--><div class="language-yaml vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">yaml</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">title</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">Exchange ProxyShell exploitation attempt in web logs</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">logsource</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  category</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">webserver</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">detection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  selection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">    c-uri|contains|all</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">      - </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;/ecp/default.aspx&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">      - </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;__VIEWSTATEGENERATOR=&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">      - </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;__VIEWSTATE=&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  condition</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">selection</span></span></code></pre></div><div class="language-splunk vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">splunk</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;c-uri&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;*/ecp/default.aspx*&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;"> &quot;c-uri&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;*__VIEWSTATEGENERATOR=*&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;"> &quot;c-uri&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;*__VIEWSTATE=*&quot;</span></span></code></pre></div><!--]--></div><!----></div><p>Normally, lists of values are linked with <code>OR</code> in the generated query.<br>The <code>all</code> modifier changes this to <code>AND</code>.</p><p>This modifier is useful if you want to express a command line invocation with different parameters where the order may vary and removes the need for some cumbersome workarounds.</p><div class="info custom-block"><p class="custom-block-title">Note:</p><p>Single item values are not allowed to have an <code>all</code> modifier as some backends cannot support it. If you use it as a workaround to duplicate a field in a selection, use a new selection instead.</p></div><hr><h3 id="base64-base64offset" tabindex="-1">base64 / base64offset <a class="header-anchor" href="#base64-base64offset" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;base64 / base64offset&quot;">​</a></h3><div class="sigma-converter not-prose my-8" data-v-b4727905><div class="sigma-converter-static" style="" data-v-b4727905><!--[--><div class="language-yaml vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">yaml</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">title</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">Base64 shell usage in HTTP web traffic</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">logsource</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  product</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">linux</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">detection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  selection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">    fieldname|base64offset|contains</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">      - </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">/bin/bash</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">      - </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">/bin/sh</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">      - </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">/bin/zsh</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  condition</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">selection</span></span></code></pre></div><div class="language-splunk vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">splunk</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">fieldname</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;*L2Jpbi9iYXNo*&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> OR</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;"> fieldname</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;*9iaW4vYmFza*&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> OR</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;"> fieldname</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;*vYmluL2Jhc2*&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> OR</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;"> fieldname</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;*L2Jpbi9za*&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> OR</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;"> fieldname</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;*9iaW4vc2*&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> OR</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;"> fieldname</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;*vYmluL3No*&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> OR</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;"> fieldname</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;*L2Jpbi96c2*&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> OR</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;"> fieldname</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;*9iaW4venNo*&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> OR</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;"> fieldname</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;*vYmluL3pza*&quot;</span></span></code></pre></div><!--]--></div><!----></div><p>The <code>base64</code> modifier-set will encode the provided values as base64 encoded strings. Often used alongside <code>contains</code> to identify malicious injection into applications.</p><p>This technique is often used by malicious actors to hide behaviour by executing commands, or sending HTTP parameters, using base64, sometimes preventing traditional detection methods.</p><div class="tip custom-block"><p class="custom-block-title">Tip:</p><p>The <code>base64offset</code> modifier is usually preferred over the <code>base64</code> modifier, because an ASCII value encoded into <code>base64</code> can have 3 different offsets (or shifts) that can occur when completing the encoding process.</p></div><hr><h3 id="cased" tabindex="-1">cased <a class="header-anchor" href="#cased" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;cased&quot;">​</a></h3><div class="sigma-converter not-prose my-8" data-v-b4727905><div class="sigma-converter-static" style="" data-v-b4727905><!--[--><div class="language-yaml vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">yaml</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">title</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">Example of cased modifier</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">logsource</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  product</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">example</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">detection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  selection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">    fieldname|cased</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;CaseSensitiveValue&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  condition</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">selection</span></span></code></pre></div><div class="language-sql vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">sql</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">SELECT</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> *</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> FROM</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> &lt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">TABLE_NAME</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> WHERE</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> fieldname GLOB </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&#39;CaseSensitiveValue&#39;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> ESCAPE </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&#39;\&#39;</span></span></code></pre></div><!--]--></div><!----></div><p>The <code>cased</code> modifier indicates that the value is applied in a case-sensitive manner. Sigma&#39;s default behavior is case-insensitive matching.</p><div class="warning custom-block"><p class="custom-block-title">Not every backend supports case-sensitive matching</p><p>Some query languages — including Splunk SPL and Elasticsearch — have no native case-sensitive operator, so the <code>cased</code> modifier produces no additional query constraint there. Backends like SQL (<code>GLOB</code>) and Grafana Loki do honour it, which is why this example is restricted to those targets.</p></div><hr><h3 id="cidr" tabindex="-1">cidr <a class="header-anchor" href="#cidr" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;cidr&quot;">​</a></h3><div class="sigma-converter not-prose my-8" data-v-b4727905><div class="sigma-converter-static" style="" data-v-b4727905><!--[--><div class="language-yaml vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">yaml</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">title</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">Example of cidr modifier with IPv4 subnets</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">logsource</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  product</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">example</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">detection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  selection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">    first_ip_address|cidr</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">192.0.0.0/8</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">    second_ip_address|cidr</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">192.168.0.0/23</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  condition</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">selection</span></span></code></pre></div><div class="language-splunk vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">splunk</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">first_ip_address</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;192.0.0.0/8&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;"> second_ip_address</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;192.168.0.0/23&quot;</span></span></code></pre></div><!--]--></div><!----></div><div class="sigma-converter not-prose my-8" data-v-b4727905><div class="sigma-converter-static" style="" data-v-b4727905><!--[--><div class="language-yaml vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">yaml</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">title</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">Example of cidr modifier with an IPv6 subnet</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">logsource</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  product</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">example</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">detection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  selection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">    ipaddress|cidr</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">2a03:2880:f132:83:face:b00c::/96</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  condition</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">selection</span></span></code></pre></div><div class="language-splunk vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">splunk</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">ipaddress</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;2a03:2880:f132:83:face:b00c::/96&quot;</span></span></code></pre></div><!--]--></div><!----></div><p>The <code>cidr</code> modifier allows for CIDR-formatted subnets to be used as field values, where any IPv4 or IPv6 addresses are supported.</p><hr><h3 id="contains" tabindex="-1">contains <a class="header-anchor" href="#contains" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;contains&quot;">​</a></h3><div class="sigma-converter not-prose my-8" data-v-b4727905><div class="sigma-converter-static" style="" data-v-b4727905><!--[--><div class="language-yaml vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">yaml</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">title</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">Example of contains modifier</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">logsource</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  product</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">example</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">detection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  selection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">    fieldname|contains</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">needle</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  condition</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">selection</span></span></code></pre></div><div class="language-splunk vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">splunk</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">fieldname</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;*needle*&quot;</span></span></code></pre></div><!--]--></div><!----></div><p>The <code>contains</code> modifier will insert a wildcard token (usually <code>*</code>) around the provided value(s), such that the value is matched anywhere in the field.</p><hr><h3 id="endswith" tabindex="-1">endswith <a class="header-anchor" href="#endswith" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;endswith&quot;">​</a></h3><div class="sigma-converter not-prose my-8" data-v-b4727905><div class="sigma-converter-static" style="" data-v-b4727905><!--[--><div class="language-yaml vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">yaml</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">title</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">Example of endswith modifier</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">logsource</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  product</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">example</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">detection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  selection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">    fieldname|endswith</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">needle</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  condition</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">selection</span></span></code></pre></div><div class="language-splunk vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">splunk</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">fieldname</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;*needle&quot;</span></span></code></pre></div><!--]--></div><!----></div><p>The <code>endswith</code> modifier will insert a wildcard token (usually <code>*</code>) at the start of the provided value(s), such that the value is matched at the end of the field.</p><hr><h3 id="exists" tabindex="-1">exists <a class="header-anchor" href="#exists" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;exists&quot;">​</a></h3><div class="sigma-converter not-prose my-8" data-v-b4727905><div class="sigma-converter-static" style="" data-v-b4727905><!--[--><div class="language-yaml vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">yaml</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">title</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">Administrator Usage</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">logsource</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  product</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">windows</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">detection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  selection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">    user|exists</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">true</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  condition</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">selection</span></span></code></pre></div><div class="language-text vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">text</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span>user exists</span></span></code></pre></div><!--]--></div><!----></div><div class="sigma-converter not-prose my-8" data-v-b4727905><div class="sigma-converter-static" style="" data-v-b4727905><!--[--><div class="language-yaml vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">yaml</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">title</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">Administrator Usage</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">logsource</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  product</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">windows</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">detection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  selection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">    user|exists</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">false</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  condition</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">selection</span></span></code></pre></div><div class="language-text vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">text</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span>user !exists</span></span></code></pre></div><!--]--></div><!----></div><p>The <code>exists</code> modifier will generate a query to check if <code>fieldname</code> exists. The value for the modifier can either be <code>true</code> or <code>false</code>. Setting the value to <code>false</code> will result in a not exists query.</p><hr><h3 id="expand" tabindex="-1">expand <a class="header-anchor" href="#expand" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;expand&quot;">​</a></h3><div class="sigma-converter not-prose my-8" data-v-b4727905><div class="sigma-converter-static" style="" data-v-b4727905><!--[--><div class="vp-code-group vp-adaptive-theme"><div class="tabs"><input type="radio" name="group-Fra1g" id="tab-XIOat4_" checked><label data-title="pipelines/value_placeholders_test.yml" for="tab-XIOat4_">pipelines/value_placeholders_test.yml</label><input type="radio" name="group-Fra1g" id="tab-FAn57dt"><label data-title="rules/rule.yml" for="tab-FAn57dt">rules/rule.yml</label></div><div class="blocks"><div class="language-yaml vp-adaptive-theme active"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">yaml</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">name</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">value_placeholder_pipeline</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">vars</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  administrator_name</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">Administrator</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">transformations</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">  - </span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">type</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">value_placeholders</span></span></code></pre></div><div class="language-yaml vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">yaml</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">title</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">Administrator Usage</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">logsource</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  product</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">windows</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">detection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  selection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">    user|expand</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;%administrator_name%&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  condition</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">selection</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><div class="language-splunk vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">splunk</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">user</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;Administrator&quot;</span></span></code></pre></div><!--]--></div><!----></div><p>The <code>expand</code> modifier can be used with Sigma Pipelines in order to replace placeholder values with another value common across that processing pipeline.</p><hr><h3 id="fieldref" tabindex="-1">fieldref <a class="header-anchor" href="#fieldref" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;fieldref&quot;">​</a></h3><div class="sigma-converter not-prose my-8" data-v-b4727905><div class="sigma-converter-static" style="" data-v-b4727905><!--[--><div class="language-yaml vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">yaml</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">title</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">Example of fieldref modifier</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">logsource</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  product</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">example</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">detection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  selection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">    fieldname|fieldref</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">fieldasString</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  condition</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">selection</span></span></code></pre></div><div class="language-splunk vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">splunk</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">*</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">|</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> where</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;"> &#39;fieldname&#39;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&#39;fieldasString&#39;</span></span></code></pre></div><!--]--></div><!----></div><p>The <code>fieldref</code> mofidier will convert a plain string into a field reference. <code>fieldname</code> and <code>fieldasString</code> must have the same value. A field reference can be used to compare fields of matched events directly at query/matching time.</p><hr><h3 id="gt" tabindex="-1">gt <a class="header-anchor" href="#gt" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;gt&quot;">​</a></h3><div class="sigma-converter not-prose my-8" data-v-b4727905><div class="sigma-converter-static" style="" data-v-b4727905><!--[--><div class="language-yaml vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">yaml</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">title</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">Example of gt modifier</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">logsource</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  product</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">example</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">detection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  selection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">    fieldname|gt</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">15</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  condition</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">selection</span></span></code></pre></div><div class="language-splunk vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">splunk</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">fieldname&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">15</span></span></code></pre></div><!--]--></div><!----></div><p>The <code>gt</code> modifier will provide a search where the value of <code>fieldname</code> is greater than the value provided.</p><hr><h3 id="gte" tabindex="-1">gte <a class="header-anchor" href="#gte" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;gte&quot;">​</a></h3><div class="sigma-converter not-prose my-8" data-v-b4727905><div class="sigma-converter-static" style="" data-v-b4727905><!--[--><div class="language-yaml vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">yaml</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">title</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">Example of gte modifier</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">logsource</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  product</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">example</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">detection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  selection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">    fieldname|gte</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">15</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  condition</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">selection</span></span></code></pre></div><div class="language-splunk vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">splunk</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">fieldname&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">15</span></span></code></pre></div><!--]--></div><!----></div><p>The <code>gte</code> modifier will provide a search where the value of <code>fieldname</code> is greater than or equal to the value provided.</p><hr><h3 id="lt" tabindex="-1">lt <a class="header-anchor" href="#lt" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;lt&quot;">​</a></h3><div class="sigma-converter not-prose my-8" data-v-b4727905><div class="sigma-converter-static" style="" data-v-b4727905><!--[--><div class="language-yaml vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">yaml</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">title</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">Example of lt modifier</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">logsource</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  product</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">example</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">detection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  selection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">    fieldname|lt</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">15</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  condition</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">selection</span></span></code></pre></div><div class="language-splunk vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">splunk</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">fieldname&lt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">15</span></span></code></pre></div><!--]--></div><!----></div><p>The <code>lt</code> modifier will provide a search where the value of <code>fieldname</code> is less than the value provided.</p><hr><h3 id="lte" tabindex="-1">lte <a class="header-anchor" href="#lte" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;lte&quot;">​</a></h3><div class="sigma-converter not-prose my-8" data-v-b4727905><div class="sigma-converter-static" style="" data-v-b4727905><!--[--><div class="language-yaml vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">yaml</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">title</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">Example of lte modifier</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">logsource</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  product</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">example</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">detection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  selection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">    fieldname|lte</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">15</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  condition</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">selection</span></span></code></pre></div><div class="language-splunk vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">splunk</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">fieldname&lt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">15</span></span></code></pre></div><!--]--></div><!----></div><p>The <code>lte</code> modifier will provide a search where the value of <code>fieldname</code> is less than or equal to the value provided.</p><hr><h3 id="re" tabindex="-1">re <a class="header-anchor" href="#re" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;re&quot;">​</a></h3><div class="sigma-converter not-prose my-8" data-v-b4727905><div class="sigma-converter-static" style="" data-v-b4727905><!--[--><div class="language-yaml vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">yaml</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">title</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">Example of re (regex) modifier</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">logsource</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  product</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">example</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">detection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  selection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">    fieldname|re</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">.*needle$</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  condition</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">selection</span></span></code></pre></div><div class="language-splunk vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">splunk</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">*</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">|</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> regex</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;"> fieldname</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;.*needle$&quot;</span></span></code></pre></div><!--]--></div><!----></div><p>The <code>re</code> modifier will provide a search where the value of <code>fieldname</code> matches the provided regex.</p><p>There are re sub-modifiers <code>re|?</code>:</p><ul><li><code>i</code>: (insensitive) to enable case-insensitive matching.</li><li><code>m</code>: (multi line) to match across multiple lines. <code>^</code>/<code>$</code> match the start/end of line.</li><li><code>s</code>: (single line) to enable that dot (.) matches all characters, including the newline character.</li></ul><hr><h3 id="startswith" tabindex="-1">startswith <a class="header-anchor" href="#startswith" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;startswith&quot;">​</a></h3><div class="sigma-converter not-prose my-8" data-v-b4727905><div class="sigma-converter-static" style="" data-v-b4727905><!--[--><div class="language-yaml vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">yaml</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">title</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">Example of startswith modifier</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">logsource</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  product</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">example</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">detection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  selection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">    fieldname|startswith</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">needle</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  condition</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">selection</span></span></code></pre></div><div class="language-splunk vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">splunk</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">fieldname</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;needle*&quot;</span></span></code></pre></div><!--]--></div><!----></div><p>The <code>startswith</code> modifier will insert a wildcard token (usually <code>*</code>) at the end of the provided value(s), such that the value is matched at the beginning of the field.</p><hr><h3 id="wide" tabindex="-1">utf16 / utf16le / utf16be / wide <a class="header-anchor" href="#wide" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;utf16 / utf16le / utf16be / wide {#wide}&quot;">​</a></h3><div class="sigma-converter not-prose my-8" data-v-b4727905><div class="sigma-converter-static" style="" data-v-b4727905><!--[--><div class="language-yaml vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">yaml</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">title</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">Example of wide (utf16) modifier</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">logsource</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  product</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">example</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">detection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  selection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">    CommandLine|wide|base64offset|contains</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;ping&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  condition</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">selection</span></span></code></pre></div><div class="language-splunk vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">splunk</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">CommandLine</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;*cABpAG4AZw*&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> OR</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;"> CommandLine</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;*AAaQBuAGcA*&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> OR</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;"> CommandLine</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;*wAGkAbgBnA*&quot;</span></span></code></pre></div><!--]--></div><!----></div><p>Prepends a byte order mark and encodes UTF16, (only used in combination with base64 modifiers)</p><div class="warning custom-block"><p class="custom-block-title">Don&#39;t end with <code>utf16</code>, <code>utf16le</code>, <code>utf16be</code> or <code>wide</code></p><p>The value modifier chain must not end with character set encoding modifiers (<code>utf16</code>, <code>utf16le</code>, <code>utf16be</code> and <code>wide</code>). The resulting values are internally represented as byte sequences instead of text strings and contain null characters which are usually difficult to handle in queries. Therefore the should be followed by an encoding modifier (base64, base64offset)</p></div><hr><h3 id="windash" tabindex="-1">windash <a class="header-anchor" href="#windash" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;windash&quot;">​</a></h3><div class="sigma-converter not-prose my-8" data-v-b4727905><div class="sigma-converter-static" style="" data-v-b4727905><!--[--><div class="language-yaml vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">yaml</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">title</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">Example of windash modifier</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">logsource</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  product</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">example</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">detection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  selection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">    fieldname|windash|contains</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">      - </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot; -param-name &quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">      - </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot; -f &quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  condition</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">selection</span></span></code></pre></div><div class="language-splunk vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">splunk</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">fieldname</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;* -param-name *&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> OR</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;"> fieldname</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;* /param-name *&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> OR</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;"> fieldname</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;* –param-name *&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> OR</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;"> fieldname</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;* —param-name *&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> OR</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;"> fieldname</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;* ―param-name *&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> OR</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;"> fieldname</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;* -f *&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> OR</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;"> fieldname</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;* /f *&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> OR</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;"> fieldname</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;* –f *&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> OR</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;"> fieldname</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;* —f *&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> OR</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;"> fieldname</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;* ―f *&quot;</span></span></code></pre></div><!--]--></div><!----></div><p>The windash modifier will convert any provided command-line arguments or flags to use <code>-</code>, as well as <code>/</code>, <code>–</code> (En Dash), <code>—</code> (Em Dash), and <code>―</code> (Horizontal Bar).</p><p>This is incredibly useful in the the Windows ecosystem, where Windows has <a href="https://learn.microsoft.com/en-us/powershell/scripting/learn/shell/running-commands?view=powershell-7.3#passing-arguments-to-native-commands" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer">two standards for passing arguments to commands</a>, usually <code>-</code> for PowerShell (e.g. <code>-a</code>), and <code>/</code> for <code>cmd.exe</code> (e.g. <code>/a</code>), but a large number of commands will commonly accept both. Many tools, including PowerShell, will not only accept a normal hyphen, but other similar looking dashes like <code>–</code> (En Dash), <code>—</code> (Em Dash), and <code>―</code> (Horizontal Bar)</p><hr></div></div></main><footer class="VPDocFooter" data-v-e6f2a212 data-v-1bcd8184><!--[--><!--]--><div class="edit-info" data-v-1bcd8184><div class="edit-link" data-v-1bcd8184><a class="VPLink link vp-external-link-icon no-icon edit-link-button" href="https://github.com/SigmaHQ/sigmahq.github.io/edit/main/docs/basics/modifiers.md" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" data-v-1bcd8184><!--[--><span class="vpi-square-pen edit-link-icon" data-v-1bcd8184></span> Edit on GitHub<!--]--></a></div><div class="last-updated" data-v-1bcd8184><p class="VPLastUpdated" data-v-1bcd8184 data-v-1bb0c8a8>Last updated: <time datetime="2026-06-15T18:22:29.000Z" data-v-1bb0c8a8></time></p></div></div><nav class="prev-next" aria-labelledby="doc-footer-aria-label" data-v-1bcd8184><span class="visually-hidden" id="doc-footer-aria-label" data-v-1bcd8184>Pager</span><div class="pager" data-v-1bcd8184><a class="VPLink link pager-link prev" href="/docs/basics/rules.html" data-v-1bcd8184><!--[--><span class="desc" data-v-1bcd8184>Previous page</span><span class="title" data-v-1bcd8184>Rules</span><!--]--></a></div><div class="pager" data-v-1bcd8184><a class="VPLink link pager-link next" href="/docs/basics/conditions.html" data-v-1bcd8184><!--[--><span class="desc" data-v-1bcd8184>Next page</span><span class="title" data-v-1bcd8184>Conditions</span><!--]--></a></div></nav></footer><!--[--><!--]--></div></div></div><!--[--><!--]--></div></div><footer class="VPFooter has-sidebar" data-v-d8b57b2d data-v-566314d4><div class="container" data-v-566314d4><!----><p class="copyright" data-v-566314d4>Copyright © 2020-present SigmaHQ</p></div></footer><!--[--><!--]--></div></div>

content</a><!--]--><!----><header class="VPNav" data-v-d8b57b2d data-v-7ad780c2><div class="VPNavBar" data-v-7ad780c2 data-v-9fd4d1dd><div class="wrapper" data-v-9fd4d1dd><div class="container" data-v-9fd4d1dd><div class="title" data-v-9fd4d1dd><div class="VPNavBarTitle has-sidebar" data-v-9fd4d1dd data-v-9f43907a><a class="title" href="/" Taxonomy Appendix</p><!--]--></a><!----></div><!----></div><div class="VPSidebarItem level-1 is-link" data-v-0009425e data-v-0009425e><div class="item" data-v-0009425e><div class="indicator" data-v-0009425e><!--[--><p class="text" data-v-0009425e>SigmaHQ Conventions</p><!--]--></a><!----></div><!----></div><!--]--></div></section></div><!--]--><!--[--><!--[--><div class="block w-full border-t border-[var(--vp-c-divider)] pt-6 text-xs text-slate-400 transition-all dark:text-slate-700"><div class="mb-0.5 font-semibold"> Copyright © <a href="https://sigmahq.io/">SigmaHQ</a>
