target="_blank">Discord</a></div></div><!--]--><!--]--></nav></aside><div class="VPContent has-sidebar" id="VPContent" data-v-d8b57b2d data-v-9a6c75ad><div class="VPDoc has-sidebar has-aside" data-v-9a6c75ad data-v-e6f2a212><!--[--><!--]--><div class="container" data-v-e6f2a212><div class="aside" data-v-e6f2a212><div class="aside-curtain" data-v-e6f2a212></div><div class="aside-container" data-v-e6f2a212><div class="aside-content" data-v-e6f2a212><div class="VPDocAside" data-v-e6f2a212 data-v-cb998dce><!--[--><!--]--><!--[--><!--]--><nav aria-labelledby="doc-outline-aria-label" class="VPDocAsideOutline" data-v-cb998dce data-v-f610f197><div class="content" data-v-f610f197><div class="outline-marker" data-v-f610f197></div><div aria-level="2" class="outline-title" id="doc-outline-aria-label" role="heading" data-v-f610f197>On this page</div><ul class="VPDocOutlineItem root" data-v-f610f197 data-v-53c99d69><!--[--><!--]--></ul></div></nav><!--[--><!--]--><div class="spacer" data-v-cb998dce></div><!--[--><!--]--><!----><!--[--><!--]--><!--[--><!--]--></div></div></div></div><div class="content" data-v-e6f2a212><div class="content-container" data-v-e6f2a212><!--[--><!--]--><main class="main" data-v-e6f2a212><div style="position:relative;" class="vp-doc _docs_basics_conditions" data-v-e6f2a212><div><h1 id="sigma-frontmatter-title" tabindex="-1">Sigma Conditions <a class="header-anchor" href="#sigma-frontmatter-title" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;Sigma {{ $frontmatter.title }}&quot;">​</a></h1><p>To enable Sigma to represent more complex boolean operations found in Log Query Languages (such as <code>NOT</code>, <code>AND</code>, &amp; <code>OR</code> operations), Sigma rules are equipped with a <code>condition</code> field – as part of the <code>detection</code> section. This enables Sigma detections to logically be organised into different sections, as well as perform functions like filtering for known false-positives.</p><h2 id="basic-conditions" tabindex="-1">Basic Conditions <a class="header-anchor" href="#basic-conditions" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;Basic Conditions&quot;">​</a></h2><h3 id="not" tabindex="-1">not <a class="header-anchor" href="#not" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;not&quot;">​</a></h3><p>The <code>not</code> expression allows the completion of an inverse search.</p><p>In the example below, we&#39;re searching for all events where the <code>id.orig_h</code> (Connecting IP) IP address does not come from an internal network.</p><div class="sigma-converter not-prose my-8" data-v-b4727905><div class="sigma-converter-static" style="" data-v-b4727905><!--[--><div class="language-yaml vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">yaml</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark has-diff vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">title</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">Connection from an external (non-internal) IP address</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">logsource</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  category</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">firewall</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">detection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  selection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">    id.orig_h|cidr</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">      - </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;10.0.0.0/8&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">      - </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;172.16.0.0/12&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">      - </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;192.168.0.0/24&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line diff add"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  condition</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">not selection</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D;">  # NOT (id.orig_h == &quot;10.*&quot; OR ... OR id.orig_h == &quot;192.168.*&quot;)</span></span></code></pre></div><div class="language-splunk vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">splunk</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">NOT</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> (</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">id.orig_h</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;10.0.0.0/8&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> OR</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;"> id.orig_h</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;172.16.0.0/12&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> OR</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;"> id.orig_h</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;192.168.0.0/24&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">)</span></span></code></pre></div><!--]--></div><!----></div><h3 id="and" tabindex="-1">and <a class="header-anchor" href="#and" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;and&quot;">​</a></h3><p>The <code>and</code> expression combines two selections into one by joining them with an <strong>AND</strong> statement.</p><div class="sigma-converter not-prose my-8" data-v-b4727905><div class="sigma-converter-static" style="" data-v-b4727905><!--[--><div class="language-yaml vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">yaml</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark has-diff vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">title</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">Setup executable accessed on a CD-ROM device</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">logsource</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  product</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">windows</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  service</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">security</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">detection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  selection_1</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">    EventID</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">4663</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  selection_2</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">    ObjectName</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&#39;\Device\CdRom0\setup.exe&#39;</span></span>
<span class="line diff add"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  condition</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">selection_1 and selection_2</span></span></code></pre></div><div class="language-splunk vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">splunk</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">EventID</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">4663</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;"> ObjectName</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;\\Device\\CdRom0\\setup.exe&quot;</span></span></code></pre></div><!--]--></div><!----></div><div class="tip custom-block"><p class="custom-block-title">Filters</p><p>You can effectively use the <code>and</code> and <code>not</code> selection conditions to filter our unwanted or known false-positives in your Sigma rule.</p><div class="sigma-converter not-prose my-8 border-2 border-[var(--vp-c-bg)]/80 rounded-xl px-2 bg-[var(--vp-c-bg)]/80" data-v-b4727905><div class="sigma-converter-static" style="" data-v-b4727905><!--[--><div class="language-yaml vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">yaml</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark has-diff vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">title</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">Bash shell with outbound network connection (excluding loopback)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">logsource</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  product</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">linux</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">detection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  selection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">    Image|endswith</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;/bin/bash&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  filter</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">    DestinationIp</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">      - </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;127.0.0.1&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">      - </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;0.0.0.0&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line diff add"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  condition</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">selection and not filter</span></span></code></pre></div><div class="language-splunk vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">splunk</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">Image</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;*/bin/bash&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> NOT</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> (DestinationIp IN (</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;127.0.0.1&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;0.0.0.0&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">))</span></span></code></pre></div><!--]--></div><!----></div></div><h3 id="or" tabindex="-1">or <a class="header-anchor" href="#or" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;or&quot;">​</a></h3><p>The <code>or</code> expression combines two selections into an &quot;either&quot; by joining them with an <strong>OR</strong> statement.</p><div class="sigma-converter not-prose my-8" data-v-b4727905><div class="sigma-converter-static" style="" data-v-b4727905><!--[--><div class="language-yaml vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">yaml</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark has-diff vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">title</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">AWS SAML provider manipulation</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">logsource</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  product</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">aws</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  service</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">cloudtrail</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">detection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  selection1</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">    eventSource</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">sts.amazonaws.com</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">    eventName</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">AssumeRoleWithSAML</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  selection2</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">    eventSource</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">iam.amazonaws.com</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">    eventName</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">UpdateSAMLProvider</span></span>

href="#brackets" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;`brackets`&quot;">​</a></h3><p>Where more complex operations need to take place, the brackets operator allows for the grouping of different operations, and will translate to use the brackets inside your detection environment.</p><p>Brackets also help remove ambiguity around order of operations between the <code>and</code>, <code>or</code> and <code>not</code> conditions.</p><div class="sigma-converter not-prose my-8" data-v-b4727905><div class="sigma-converter-static" style="" data-v-b4727905><!--[--><div class="language-yaml Taxonomy Appendix</p><!--]--></a><!----></div><!----></div><div class="VPSidebarItem level-1 is-link" data-v-0009425e data-v-0009425e><div class="item" data-v-0009425e><div class="indicator" border-t border-[var(--vp-c-divider)] pt-6 text-xs text-slate-400 transition-all dark:text-slate-700"><div class="mb-0.5 font-semibold"> Copyright © <a href="https://sigmahq.io/">SigmaHQ</a> class="hover:text-cyan-600" target="_blank">X.com</a><span class="opacity-30">|</span><a href="https://discord.gg/kQQBn5W2z5" class="hover:text-cyan-600" target="_blank">Discord</a></div></div><!--]--><!--]--></nav></aside><div class="VPContent has-sidebar" id="VPContent" data-v-d8b57b2d data-v-9a6c75ad><div class="VPDoc has-sidebar has-aside" data-v-9a6c75ad data-v-e6f2a212><!--[--><!--]--><div class="container" data-v-e6f2a212><div class="aside" data-v-e6f2a212><div class="aside-curtain" data-v-e6f2a212></div><div class="aside-container" data-v-e6f2a212><div class="aside-content" data-v-e6f2a212><div class="VPDocAside" data-v-e6f2a212 data-v-cb998dce><!--[--><!--]--><!--[--><!--]--><nav aria-labelledby="doc-outline-aria-label" class="VPDocAsideOutline" data-v-cb998dce data-v-f610f197><div class="content" data-v-f610f197><div class="outline-marker" data-v-f610f197></div><div aria-level="2" class="outline-title" id="doc-outline-aria-label" role="heading" data-v-f610f197>On this page</div><ul class="VPDocOutlineItem root" data-v-f610f197 data-v-53c99d69><!--[--><!--]--></ul></div></nav><!--[--><!--]--><div class="spacer" data-v-cb998dce></div><!--[--><!--]--><!----><!--[--><!--]--><!--[--><!--]--></div></div></div></div><div class="content" data-v-e6f2a212><div class="content-container" data-v-e6f2a212><!--[--><!--]--><main class="main" data-v-e6f2a212><div style="position:relative;" class="vp-doc _docs_basics_log-sources" data-v-e6f2a212><div><h1 id="frontmatter-title" tabindex="-1">Logsources <a class="header-anchor" href="#frontmatter-title" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;{{ $frontmatter.title }}&quot;">​</a></h1><p>For each <a href="/docs/basics/rules.html">Sigma rule</a> to be effective at detection, it is important to identify what type of logs your SIEM is required to search over. This is important not only for efficiency of detections, but also for ensuring detection is happening against the correct set of fields and values applied.</p><p>Each logsource definition within a Sigma rule is made up of <strong>three</strong> separate fields. These fields, when used in combination, define a given logsource.</p><ul><li><code>category</code></li><li><code>product</code></li><li><code>service</code></li></ul><p>Each Sigma logsource is then usually (depending on your SIEM) prepended to the start of a detection query, in order for that query to target only those specific set of logs relevant to that detection. See this example below:</p><h2 id="logsource-basics" tabindex="-1">Logsource Basics <a class="header-anchor" href="#logsource-basics" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;Logsource Basics&quot;">​</a></h2><p>Before Sigma queries can be used effectively within an organization&#39;s SIEM or Alerting tooling, it&#39;s important to identify whether the detection can search over the appropriate types of logs that the Sigma detection requires.</p><p>Because each logsource will look fairly similar – especially in Sigma rules targeting Microsoft Windows™ domain – it&#39;s important to know when Sigma rules will match again a logsource, as any mismatches in logsource can render the detection ineffective.</p><div class="info custom-block"><p class="custom-block-title">Sigma Specification for Logsources</p><p>The Sigma Specification repository outlines a <a href="https://github.com/SigmaHQ/sigma-specification/blob/main/specification/sigma-appendix-taxonomy.md#log-sources" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer">standard set of logsources</a>, that is supported across the community in the Sigma rule collection.</p></div><h3 id="logsource-types" tabindex="-1">Logsource Types <a class="header-anchor" href="#logsource-types" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;Logsource Types&quot;">​</a></h3><p>The <code>category</code> value is used to select all log files written by a certain group of products, like firewalls or web server logs.</p><p>The <code>product</code> value is used to select all log outputs of a certain product. For example, all Windows Eventlog types including &quot;Security&quot;, &quot;System&quot;, &quot;Application&quot; and the new log types like &quot;AppLocker&quot; and &quot;Windows Defender&quot;.</p><p>Use the <code>service</code> value to select only a subset of a product&#39;s logs, like the &quot;sshd&quot; on Linux or the &quot;Security&quot; Eventlog on Windows systems.</p><h3 id="definition-field" tabindex="-1">Definition Field <a class="header-anchor" href="#definition-field" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;Definition Field&quot;">​</a></h3><p>You may also see a <code>definition</code> field within logsource description. This can also provide more information about how to onboard the log data source correctly, and doesn&#39;t get included when completing logsource matching.</p><div class="language-yaml vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">yaml</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark has-focused-lines vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">tags</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">  - </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">attack.privilege_escalation</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">  - </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">attack.t1548</span></span>
<span class="line has-focus"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">logsource</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span></span>
<span class="line has-focus"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  product</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">windows</span></span>
<span class="line has-focus"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  category</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">ps_script</span></span>
<span class="line highlighted has-focus"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  definition</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">Script Block Logging must be enabled</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">detection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">  selection</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D;">    ScriptBlockText|contains</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&#39;Invoke-Nightmare&#39;</span></span></code></pre></div><h2 id="available-logsources" tabindex="-1">Available Logsources <a class="header-anchor" href="#available-logsources" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;Available Logsources&quot;">​</a></h2><h3 id="standard-logsources" tabindex="-1">Standard Logsources <a class="header-anchor" href="#standard-logsources" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;Standard Logsources&quot;">​</a></h3><p>Below is a list of standard Sigma logsources.   category: process_creation
  product: macos</span></span></code></pre></div></div><!--]--><h3 id="custom-logsources" tabindex="-1">Custom Logsources <a class="header-anchor" href="#custom-logsources" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;Custom Logsources&quot;">​</a></h3><p>Sigma does not restrict what a Sigma logsource can be defined as, meaning you can use Sigma for just about any kind of logsource within your SIEM.</p><p>With the use of <a href="/docs/digging-deeper/pipelines.html">Pipelines</a>, you can specify granular field-mapping, and logsource-mapping to ensure that your Sigma rules are correct right
